08-03-2021 01:52:55 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100 AND `mauta_automat` = '1'

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29426-skocv_14'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

08-03-2021 01:57:25 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

08-03-2021 02:00:22 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID)

08-03-2021 02:00:27 {"title":"auto 29859 MBVIT_08","id":null,"content":"Vito Tourer 119BlueTEC VTS\/L","url":null,"image":"","meta":{"mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l":"1030","mauta_druh-phm":"Nafta","mauta_pocet-sedadel":"8","mauta_pohanena-naprava":"Zadn\u00ed","mauta_rok-vyroby":"2019","mauta_cenaden":"100","mauta_automat":"1"}}
08-03-2021 02:00:29 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

08-03-2021 02:01:50 {"title":"auto 29956 SKRAP_29RISK","id":null,"content":"Rapid Liftback 1.0TSI AT Style","url":null,"image":"\/wp-content\/uploads\/2021\/03\/SkodaRapid.jpg","meta":{"mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l":"384","mauta_druh-phm":"Benz\u00edn","mauta_pocet-sedadel":"5","mauta_pohanena-naprava":"P\u0159edn\u00ed","mauta_rok-vyroby":"2019","mauta_cenaden":"100","mauta_automat":"1"}}
08-03-2021 02:01:52 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

08-03-2021 02:10:41 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29426-skocv_14'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29426-skocv_14'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29426-skocv_14'

08-03-2021 02:45:28 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29426-skocv_14'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

08-03-2021 02:51:11 {"title":"auto 29859 MBVIT_08","id":null,"content":"Vito Tourer 119BlueTEC VTS\/L","url":null,"image":"","meta":{"mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l":"1030","mauta_druh-phm":"Nafta","mauta_pocet-sedadel":"8","mauta_pohanena-naprava":"Zadn\u00ed","mauta_rok-vyroby":"2019","mauta_cenaden":"100","mauta_automat":"1"}}
08-03-2021 02:51:14 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-28782-fiduc_09'

08-03-2021 02:57:03 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29863-skrap_28risk'

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

08-03-2021 03:09:01 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29863-skrap_28risk'

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29863-skrap_28risk'

		SELECT post_title,post_content,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29864-skrap_28risk'
